    "#Messwerte\n",
    "\n",
    "f = np.array([3.0,6.0,9.0,12.0,15.0]) #Frequenz f[Hz]\n",
    "f_err = 0.2\n",
    "\n",
    "U = np.array([1.88,4.02,6.08,8.10,10.2]) #Induzierte Scheitelspannung U[V]\n",
    "U_err = 0.1\n",
    "\n",
    "def fit_func1(x,m): #Fitfunktion\n",
    "    return m*x  \n",
    "\n",
    "plt.errorbar(f, U, xerr = f_err, yerr = U_err, ls = \"none\", label = \"Messwerte\")\n",
    "\n",
    "val1, err1 = fit(fit_func1,f, U, sigma = U_err, absolute_sigma = True)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.plot(f,fit_func1(f,*val1),label=\"Linear Fit y = m*x \\n m = {:.5f} ¬± {:.5f}\".format(val1[0],np.sqrt(err1[0][0])))\n",
    "plt.title(\"Diagr. 1.1: $U_{max}(f)$ bei $I$ = (4.0 ¬± 0.1) A\")\n",
    "plt.xlabel(\"Frequenz $f[Hz]$\")\n",
    "plt.ylabel(\"$U_{max}[V]$\")\n",
    "plt.legend(loc = \"best\")\n",
    "plt.grid()\n",
    "plt.savefig('Diagr.1_Umax.jpeg', format = 'jpeg', dpi = 600)"
   ]

    "#Messwerte\n",
    "\n",
    "I = np.array([0.50,1.0, 1.5 ,2.0,2.5,3.0,3.5,4.0,4.5]) #Spulenstrom I[A]\n",
    "I_err = 0.01\n",
    "\n",
    "U = np.array([1.06,1.94,2.78,3.68,4.52,5.40,6.28,7.12,8.00])\n",
    "U_err = 0.1\n",
    "\n",
    "def fit_func2(a,x): #Fitfunktion\n",
    "    return a*x\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.errorbar(I, U, xerr = I_err,yerr = U_err, ls = \"none\", label = \"Messwerte\")\n",
    "\n",
    "val2, err2 = fit(fit_func2,I, U, sigma = U_err, absolute_sigma = True)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.plot(I,fit_func2(I, *val2), label = \"Linear Fit y = a*x \\na = {:.5f} ¬± {:.5f}\".format(val2[0],err2[0][0]))\n",
    "plt.title(\"Diagr. 1.2: $U_{max}$ in Abh√§ngigkeit des Spulenstroms I\")\n",
    "plt.xlabel(\"Spulenstrom $I[A]$\")\n",
    "plt.ylabel(\"$U_{max}[V]$\")\n",
    "plt.legend(loc=\"best\")\n",
    "plt.grid()\n",
    "plt.savefig('Diagr.1.2_Umax(I).jpeg', format = 'jpeg', dpi = 600)"
   ]

   "source": [
    "f, I_H, U_ind, U_H = np.loadtxt('/home/jan/Dokumente/SS 2018/PAP 2.2/V245/datasheet1.dat', unpack = True, skiprows = 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "f_err = 0.05*f #Fehler d. Wechselspannungsfrequenz: 5%\n",
    "U_H_err = 20 #Fehler U_H_err = 0.04V der Spannung in der Helmholtzspule\n",
    "I_H_err = 0.01 #Fehler I_H_err = 0.01mA des Stroms in der Helmholtzspule\n",
    "U_ind_err = 10 #Fehler U_ind_err = 0.04V d. induzierten Spannung\n",
    "\n",
    "U = U_ind/U_H #Beides pp-Spannung f√ºr Verh√§ltnis ist es egal ob pp oder rms \n",
    "U_err = U*np.sqrt((U_ind_err/U_ind)**2+(U_H_err/U_H)**2)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.title(\"Diagr. 2.2: $\\\\frac{U_{ind}}{U_{H}}$ in Abh√§ngigkeit der Frequenz $f$\")\n",
    "plt.errorbar(f,U,xerr = f_err,yerr = U_err,ls = \"none\",label = \"Messwerte\")\n",
    "plt.xlabel(\"Frequenz $f[Hz]$\")\n",
    "plt.xlim([0,2200])\n",
    "plt.ylabel(\"Verh√§ltnis $\\\\frac{U_{ind}}{U_{H}}$\")\n",
    "plt.legend(loc=\"best\", prop = {'size': 12})\n",
    "plt.grid()\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.savefig('Diagr.2.2_U(f).jpeg', format = 'jpeg', dpi = 600)"

    "plt.plot(f,fit_func1(f,*popt),label = \"Linear Fit y=m*x\\nm = ({:.5f} ¬± {:.5f})\".format(popt[0],np.sqrt(perr[0][0])))\n",
    "plt.title(\"Diagr. 2.3: Widerstand R der Spule in Abh. der Frequenz $f$\")\n",
    "plt.xlabel(\"Frequenz $f[Hz]$\")\n",
    "plt.ylabel(\"$R[\\Omega]$\")\n",
    "plt.legend(loc=\"best\", prop = {'size': 12})\n",
    "\n",
    "print('m =', popt[0], '¬±', np.sqrt(perr[0][0]))\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "L_err = np.sqrt(perr[0][0])/(2*np.pi)\n",
    "print('Induktivit√§t: L = ({:.2f} ¬± {:.2f})mH'.format(popt[0]*10**3/(2*np.pi),np.sqrt(perr[0][0])*10**3))\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.savefig('Diagr.2.3_R(f).jpeg', format = 'jpeg', dpi = 600)"
